                    // Roma version
                    $('.trending-bar__link').addClass('trending-link--truncate');
                }
    
                if ('tomatometer' === slotName) {
                    if (eo.size[0] == 524 && eo.size[1] == 40) {
                        //Increase score panel margin
                        $('#scorePanel').css('margin-bottom', '20px');
                    }
                    // Only show Tomatometer Sponsorship div if rendered
                    $('#tomatometer_sponsorship_ad').show();
                }
            }
        });

Your Ticket Confirmation # is located under the header in your email that reads "Your Ticket Reservation Details". Just below that it reads "Ticket Confirmation#:" followed by a 10-digit number. This 10-digit number is your confirmation number.
            </p>
            <p class="amc-help-drawer__copy">
                Your AMC Ticket Confirmation# can be found in your order confirmation email.
            </p>
            <img class="amc-help-drawer__icon" src="/assets/pizza-pie/images/amc_help_icon.986b4076eb0.png"
                alt="Picture of a phone screen with the AMC ticket confirmation email.
                The header reads: 'Your Ticket Reservation Details'. The line below
                it reads: 'Ticket Confirmation#' followed by a ten-digit number. The
                ten-digit number is your ticket confirmation number.  ">
        </div>
    </div>
</aside>

    </div>

        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

                When the woodworker Geppetto (Christian Rub) sees a falling star, he wishes that the puppet he just finished, Pinocchio (Dickie Jones), could become a real boy. In the night, the Blue Fairy (Evelyn Venable) grants Geppetto's wish and asks Jiminy Cricket (Cliff Edwards) to serve as the wooden boy's conscience. <section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Pinocchio</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Aug 13, 2020</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">I&#39;m torn with this movie.  On the one hand, it really takes the techniques learned by Disney during their shorts and over the course of Snow White to the next level with some truly stunning visuals.  There&#39;s a great sense of depth, and gorgeous environments.  It&#39;s one of the last films of its era, the last story-based full-length narrative before the World War II package films.  I mean, that&#39;s a very specific bar yes, but damn these things were stunning!  There&#39;s nothing quite like Disney of this era, knowing how much technique and effort was put in, the blood sweat and tears.
That being said…I do not like this movie!  I didn&#39;t like it as a kid, and I still don&#39;t.  I appreciate it historically, and I appreciate it artistically, but it&#39;s such a hopeless, sadistic little movie that it&#39;s hard to find joy in it.  It takes such sick pleasure in all the misfortune the characters go through.  There&#39;s a huge cast of sick twisted characters, and none of them get their comeuppance, so there&#39;s no sense of closure.  In some movies, that&#39;s fine, that&#39;s the point, but is this really the type of movie that should be?  And what is the point here?  Be good, follow the rules, or horrible things will happen to you and you&#39;ll never see you&#39;re loved ones again so be very afraid little children?  That&#39;s sick!  That&#39;s ugly.  That&#39;s mean!  On top of that, I don&#39;t like the characters.  Okay, I like Figaro the cat, he&#39;s got that sassy cat attitude.  Also Jiminy Cricket is more fun than I remember, he&#39;s actually kind of sarcastic and fun.  But Pinocchio is just nothing, the Blue Fairy doesn&#39;t follow her own rules, and Geppetto is a hopeless idiot and terrible father figure (case in point: I&#39;m going to take my cat and goldfish and look for my lost puppet on the ocean!).
If you get something from this story, great, cool, good for you.  To me though, it&#39;s just f***ed up, and not in a fun way.  It&#39;s happy ending isn&#39;t warranted for all the misery it puts you through and doesn&#39;t even feel deserved based on the rules they&#39;ve established.  And, like I said, there is no closure on the villains.  Again, not all films need that!  But this one really does, because good god, those are some f***ed up villains, and I needed to see the Coachman get punched in the face.  I&#39;ve tried to give this movie another chance multiple times and I just can&#39;t.  It&#39;s a gorgeous movie, technically brilliant.  There&#39;s sequences that are stunning to look at.  The whole sequence with Monstro the whale is incredible!  It&#39;s amazing to think how they did that all hand drawn and it looks just as good, if not better, than anything you could do now.  But the story is just sick, and I hate it.  Major boost in points for animation, but the story knocks it down so so much.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Michael M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Dec 15, 2012</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">I found it being rather dark, I was scared to watch it as a child. The moral lesson in the story was lost, but the animation was quite good. Not the best Disney classics, but certainly not the worst.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/892037402">
                            
                                <img class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-avatar" src="https://graph.facebook.com/v3.3/100000185301014/picture"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/892037402">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Sylvester K</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Apr 29, 2012</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Pinocchio is a great film, but compared to other Disney classics, I never really re watched this one. I on the other hand really loved the film when I saw it when I was young. This film is a must see for everyone who loves a good animated film. The film, like with every other Disney film has great art, animation and a talented voice cast. Brilliantly drawn, Pinocchio will bring out the child in every viewer and is a must see for anyone who enjoys a touching story. I loved this one growing up, but unlike other Disney classics, I never really re watched this, but I can say without a doubt that this is a near flawless film, another great one for Disney and a definite must see for the entire family. Children will love this film one, and this is a film that adults will enjoy as well. That&#39;s the beauty part about Disney films, their ability to capture the imagination of people no matter what age you are. Pinocchio is a stunning film, one that remains a Disney classic along with Snow White, Bambi and others in the company&#39;s long standing history. A very enjoyable film, Pinocchio is a memorable film that will appeal to anyone looking for a great animated film. An enjoyable ride from beginning to end, this is among Disney&#39;s very best. Brilliantly drawn, and told, Pinocchio is a terrific film that has a great story, one that will appeal to every viewer.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">

                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span></span>

                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Pinocchio is one of Walt Disney&#39;s greatest classic and one of the greatest animated films of all time.  The memory of this film lives on with all those who enjoy classic Disney animation.  This is such a great and classic film, and is one of the most beautiful works of art ever in animation.</div>
